I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[FIX] SNS Raw Message Delivery for SQS Subscriptions
## Service

SNS

## API Action / Feature

Enforce `RawMessageDelivery` subscription attribute when delivering messages to SQS subscribers.

## AWS Documentation

- https://docs.aws.amazon.com/sns/latest/dg/sns-large-payload-raw-message-delivery.html

## Why is this needed?

When `RawMessageDelivery` is set to `true` on an SQS subscription, SNS should deliver the raw message body directly to the queue — without wrapping it in the standard SNS JSON envelope. Many applications depend on this:

- Lambda functions processing SQS messages expect the raw payload, not an SNS wrapper
- Applications using SNS→SQS fanout with raw delivery parse the message body directly
- CDK patterns like `SnsEventSource` with `rawMessageDelivery: true` expect unwrapped messages

Currently, floci stores the `RawMessageDelivery` attribute but always wraps messages in the SNS envelope regardless, which means:

```json
// What the SQS consumer expects (raw):
{"orderId": "123", "status": "created"}

// What floci delivers (always wrapped):
{
  "Type": "Notification",
  "MessageId": "...",
  "TopicArn": "...",
  "Message": "{\"orderId\": \"123\", \"status\": \"created\"}",
  "Timestamp": "..."
}
```

This breaks JSON deserialization in consumers that expect the raw format.

## Expected behavior

```bash
# Setup topic and SQS queue
TOPIC_ARN=$(aws sns create-topic --name my-topic --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566 --query TopicArn --output text)
aws sqs create-queue --queue-name raw-queue --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566

# Subscribe with raw message delivery
SUB_ARN=$(aws sns subscribe --topic-arn $TOPIC_ARN --protocol sqs \
  --notification-endpoint arn:aws:sqs:us-east-1:000000000000:raw-queue \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566 --query SubscriptionArn --output text)

aws sns set-subscription-attributes --subscription-arn $SUB_ARN \
  --attribute-name RawMessageDelivery --attribute-value true \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566

# Publish a message
aws sns publish --topic-arn $TOPIC_ARN --message '{"orderId":"123"}' --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566

# Receive from SQS
aws sqs receive-message --queue-url http://localhost:4566/000000000000/raw-queue --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566

# Expected message body: {"orderId":"123"}
# Actual message body: {"Type":"Notification","MessageId":"...","Message":"{\"orderId\":\"123\"}","..."}
```

## Actual behavior

Messages are always delivered in the SNS JSON envelope regardless of the `RawMessageDelivery` setting.

## Are you willing to contribute a PR?

Yes


</pr_description>

    41	            List.of("http", "https", "email", "email-json", "sms");

    85	               LambdaService lambdaService, String baseUrl, ObjectMapper objectMapper) {

    95	    public Topic createTopic(String name, Map<String, String> attributes,
    96	                             Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
    97	        if (name == null || name.isBlank()) {
    98	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameter", "Topic name is required.", 400);
    99	        }
   100	        String topicArn = regionResolver.buildArn("sns", region, name);
   101	        String key = topicKey(region, topicArn);
   102	
   103	        Topic existing = topicStore.get(key).orElse(null);
   104	        if (existing != null) return existing;
   105	
   106	        Topic topic = new Topic(name, topicArn);
   107	        if (attributes != null) topic.getAttributes().putAll(attributes);
   108	        if (tags != null) topic.getTags().putAll(tags);
   109	
   110	        if (name.endsWith(".fifo")) {
   111	            topic.getAttributes().put("FifoTopic", "true");
   112	            topic.getAttributes().putIfAbsent("ContentBasedDeduplication", "false");
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        topicStore.put(key, topic);
   116	        LOG.infov("Created SNS topic: {0} in region {1}", name, region);
   117	        return topic;
   118	    }
   119	
   120	    public void deleteTopic(String topicArn, String region) {
   121	        String key = topicKey(region, topicArn);
   122	        if (topicStore.get(key).isEmpty()) {
   123	            throw new AwsException("NotFound", "Topic does not exist.", 404);
   124	        }
   125	        List<String> toDelete = new ArrayList<>();
   126	        String subPrefix = "sub::" + region + "::";
   127	        for (String subKey : subscriptionStore.keys()) {
   128	            if (subKey.startsWith(subPrefix)) {
   129	                subscriptionStore.get(subKey).ifPresent(sub -> {
   130	                    if (topicArn.equals(sub.getTopicArn())) toDelete.add(subKey);
   131	                });
   132	            }
   133	        }
   134	        toDelete.forEach(subscriptionStore::delete);
   135	        topicStore.delete(key);
   136	        LOG.infov("Deleted SNS topic: {0}", topicArn);
   137	    }
   138	
   139	    public List<Topic> listTopics(String region) {
   140	        String prefix = "topic::" + region + "::";
   141	        return topicStore.scan(k -> k.startsWith(prefix));
   142	    }

   144	    public Map<String, String> getTopicAttributes(String topicArn, String region) {
   145	        String key = topicKey(region, topicArn);
   146	        Topic topic = topicStore.get(key)
   147	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NotFound", "Topic does not exist.", 404));
   148	        var attrs = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>(topic.getAttributes());
   149	        List<Subscription> subs = subscriptionsByTopic(topicArn, region);
   150	        long confirmed = subs.stream()
   151	                .filter(s -> !"true".equals(s.getAttributes().get("PendingConfirmation")))
   152	                .count();
   153	        long pending = subs.stream()
   154	                .filter(s -> "true".equals(s.getAttributes().get("PendingConfirmation")))
   155	                .count();
   156	        attrs.put("SubscriptionsConfirmed", String.valueOf(confirmed));
   157	        attrs.put("SubscriptionsPending", String.valueOf(pending));
   158	        attrs.put("SubscriptionsDeleted", "0");
   159	        attrs.put("TopicArn", topicArn);
   160	        attrs.putIfAbsent("DisplayName", "");
   161	        attrs.putIfAbsent("Owner", regionResolver.getAccountId());
   162	        attrs.putIfAbsent("EffectiveDeliveryPolicy", "{\"http\":{\"defaultHealthyRetryPolicy\":{\"minDelayTarget\":20,\"maxDelayTarget\":20,\"numRetries\":3,\"numMaxDelayRetries\":0,\"numNoDelayRetries\":0,\"numMinDelayRetries\":0,\"backoffFunction\":\"linear\"},\"disableSubscriptionOverrides\":false}}");
   163	        if (!attrs.containsKey("Policy") || attrs.get("Policy") == null || attrs.get("Policy").isBlank()) {
   164	            String account = regionResolver.getAccountId();
   165	            attrs.put("Policy", "{\"Version\":\"2012-10-17\",\"Id\":\"__default_policy_ID\",\"Statement\":[{\"Sid\":\"__default_statement_ID\",\"Effect\":\"Allow\",\"Principal\":{\"AWS\":\"*\"},\"Action\":[\"SNS:GetTopicAttributes\",\"SNS:SetTopicAttributes\",\"SNS:AddPermission\",\"SNS:RemovePermission\",\"SNS:DeleteTopic\",\"SNS:Subscribe\",\"SNS:ListSubscriptionsByTopic\",\"SNS:Publish\"],\"Resource\":\"" + topicArn + "\",\"Condition\":{\"StringEquals\":{\"AWS:SourceAccount\":\"" + account + "\"}}}]}");
   166	        }
   167	        return attrs;
   168	    }

   170	    public void setTopicAttributes(String topicArn, String attributeName,
   171	                                   String attributeValue, String region) {
   172	        String key = topicKey(region, topicArn);
   173	        Topic topic = topicStore.get(key)
   174	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NotFound", "Topic does not exist.", 404));
   175	        topic.getAttributes().put(attributeName, attributeValue);
   176	        topicStore.put(key, topic);

   179	    public Subscription subscribe(String topicArn, String protocol, String endpoint, String region) {
   180	        String topicKey = topicKey(region, topicArn);
   181	        if (topicStore.get(topicKey).isEmpty()) {
   182	            throw new AwsException("NotFound", "Topic does not exist.", 404);
   183	        }
   184	        if (protocol == null || protocol.isBlank()) {
   185	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameter", "Protocol is required.", 400);
   186	        }
   187	        String subscriptionArn = topicArn + ":" + UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   188	        Subscription subscription = new Subscription(subscriptionArn, topicArn, protocol, endpoint,
   189	                regionResolver.getAccountId());
   190	
   191	        if (PENDING_CONFIRMATION_PROTOCOLS.contains(protocol)) {
   192	            String token = UUID.randomUUID().toString().replace("-", "")
   193	                    + UUID.randomUUID().toString().replace("-", "");
   194	            subscription.getAttributes().put("PendingConfirmation", "true");
   195	            subscription.getAttributes().put("ConfirmationToken", token);
   196	            LOG.infov("Subscription pending confirmation for {0} ({1}) to topic {2} in {3}",
   197	                    endpoint, protocol, topicArn, region);
   198	        }
   199	
   200	        subscriptionStore.put(subKey(region, subscriptionArn), subscription);
   201	        LOG.infov("Subscribed {0} ({1}) to topic {2} in {3}", endpoint, protocol, topicArn, region);
   202	        return subscription;
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    public String confirmSubscription(String topicArn, String token, String region) {
   206	        if (topicStore.get(topicKey(region, topicArn)).isEmpty()) {
   207	            throw new AwsException("NotFound", "Topic does not exist.", 404);
   208	        }
   209	        String subPrefix = "sub::" + region + "::";
   210	        for (String subKey : subscriptionStore.keys()) {
   211	            if (!subKey.startsWith(subPrefix)) continue;
   212	            Subscription sub = subscriptionStore.get(subKey).orElse(null);
   213	            if (sub == null || !topicArn.equals(sub.getTopicArn())) continue;
   214	            if (token.equals(sub.getAttributes().get("ConfirmationToken"))) {
   215	                sub.getAttributes().put("PendingConfirmation", "false");
   216	                sub.getAttributes().remove("ConfirmationToken");
   217	                subscriptionStore.put(subKey, sub);
   218	                LOG.infov("Confirmed subscription {0} for topic {1}", sub.getSubscriptionArn(), topicArn);
   219	                return sub.getSubscriptionArn();
   220	            }
   221	        }
   222	        throw new AwsException("AuthorizationError", "Token is invalid for this topic.", 403);
   223	    }
   224	
   225	    public void unsubscribe(String subscriptionArn, String region) {
   226	        String key = subKey(region, subscriptionArn);
   227	        if (subscriptionStore.get(key).isEmpty()) {
   228	            throw new AwsException("NotFound", "Subscription does not exist.", 404);
   229	        }
   230	        subscriptionStore.delete(key);
   231	        LOG.infov("Unsubscribed: {0}", subscriptionArn);
   232	    }

   235	        String prefix = "sub::" + region + "::";
   236	        return subscriptionStore.scan(k -> k.startsWith(prefix));
   237	    }

   253	
   254	    public String publish(String topicArn, String targetArn, String phoneNumber, String message,
   255	                          String subject, Map<String, String> messageAttributes,
   256	                          String messageGroupId, String messageDeduplicationId, String region) {
   257	        // Send SMS
   258	        if (phoneNumber != null) {
   259	            return UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   260	        }
   261	
   262	        // Send a message to topic or directly to a target ARN
   263	        String effectiveArn = topicArn != null ? topicArn : targetArn;
   264	        if (effectiveArn == null) {
   265	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameter", "TopicArn or TargetArn is required.", 400);
   266	        }
   267	        String topicStoreKey = topicKey(region, effectiveArn);
   268	        Topic topic = topicStore.get(topicStoreKey)
   269	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NotFound", "Topic does not exist.", 404));
   270	        if (message == null || message.isBlank()) {
   271	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameter", "Message is required.", 400);
   272	        }
   273	
   274	        boolean isFifo = "true".equals(topic.getAttributes().get("FifoTopic"));
   275	        if (isFifo) {
   276	            if (messageGroupId == null || messageGroupId.isBlank()) {
   277	                throw new AwsException("InvalidParameter",
   278	                        "MessageGroupId is required for FIFO topics.", 400);
   279	            }
   280	            String dedupId = messageDeduplicationId;
   281	            if (dedupId == null && "true".equals(topic.getAttributes().get("ContentBasedDeduplication"))) {
   282	                dedupId = sha256(message);
   283	            }
   284	            if (dedupId != null && isDuplicate(effectiveArn, dedupId)) {
   285	                LOG.debugv("FIFO dedup: skipping duplicate for topic {0}, dedupId {1}", effectiveArn, dedupId);
   286	                return UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   287	            }
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        String messageId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   291	        for (Subscription sub : subscriptionsByTopic(effectiveArn, region)) {
   292	            if ("true".equals(sub.getAttributes().get("PendingConfirmation"))) {
   293	                LOG.debugv("Skipping delivery to pending subscription {0}", sub.getSubscriptionArn());
   294	                continue;
   295	            }
   296	            if (!matchesFilterPolicy(sub, messageAttributes)) {
   297	                continue;
   298	            }
   299	            deliverMessage(sub, message, subject, messageAttributes, messageId, effectiveArn, messageGroupId);
   300	        }
   301	        LOG.infov("Published message {0} to topic {1}", messageId, effectiveArn);
   302	        return messageId;
   303	    }
   304	
   305	    public Map<String, String> getSubscriptionAttributes(String subscriptionArn, String region) {

   310	        attrs.put("SubscriptionArn", sub.getSubscriptionArn());
   311	        attrs.put("TopicArn", sub.getTopicArn());
   312	        attrs.put("Protocol", sub.getProtocol());
   313	        attrs.put("Endpoint", sub.getEndpoint() != null ? sub.getEndpoint() : "");
   314	        attrs.put("Owner", sub.getOwner() != null ? sub.getOwner() : "");
   315	        attrs.put("RawMessageDelivery", attrs.getOrDefault("RawMessageDelivery", "false"));
   316	        attrs.putIfAbsent("PendingConfirmation", "false");
   317	        attrs.putIfAbsent("ConfirmationWasAuthenticated", "false");
   318	        attrs.putIfAbsent("FilterPolicyScope", "MessageAttributes");

   332	    public record BatchPublishResult(List<String[]> successful, List<String[]> failed) {}
   333	
   334	    public BatchPublishResult publishBatch(String topicArn, List<Map<String, Object>> entries, String region) {
   335	        String topicStoreKey = topicKey(region, topicArn);
   336	        Topic topic = topicStore.get(topicStoreKey)
   337	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NotFound", "Topic does not exist.", 404));
   338	        boolean isFifo = "true".equals(topic.getAttributes().get("FifoTopic"));
   339	        List<String[]> successful = new ArrayList<>();
   340	        List<String[]> failed = new ArrayList<>();
   341	        for (Map<String, Object> entry : entries) {
   342	            String id = (String) entry.get("Id");
   343	            String message = (String) entry.get("Message");
   344	            if (message == null || message.isBlank()) {
   345	                failed.add(new String[]{id, "InvalidParameter", "Message is required.", "true"});
   346	                continue;
   347	            }
   348	            String subject = (String) entry.get("Subject");
   349	            String messageGroupId = (String) entry.get("MessageGroupId");
   350	            String messageDeduplicationId = (String) entry.get("MessageDeduplicationId");
   351	
   352	            if (isFifo && (messageGroupId == null || messageGroupId.isBlank())) {
   353	                failed.add(new String[]{id, "InvalidParameter",
   354	                        "MessageGroupId is required for FIFO topics.", "true"});
   355	                continue;
   356	            }
   357	            if (isFifo && messageDeduplicationId != null && isDuplicate(topicArn, messageDeduplicationId)) {
   358	                successful.add(new String[]{id, UUID.randomUUID().toString()});
   359	                continue;
   360	            }
   361	
   362	            String messageId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   363	            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   364	            Map<String, String> attrs = (Map<String, String>) entry.get("MessageAttributes");
   365	            for (Subscription sub : subscriptionsByTopic(topicArn, region)) {
   366	                if ("true".equals(sub.getAttributes().get("PendingConfirmation"))) continue;
   367	                if (!matchesFilterPolicy(sub, attrs)) continue;
   368	                deliverMessage(sub, message, subject, attrs, messageId, topicArn, messageGroupId);
   369	            }
   370	            LOG.debugv("Batch published message {0} (id={1}) to {2}", messageId, id, topicArn);
   371	            successful.add(new String[]{id, messageId});
   372	        }
   373	        return new BatchPublishResult(successful, failed);
   374	    }

   401	
   402	    /**
   403	     * Evaluates whether a message satisfies the subscription's filter policy.
   404	     * Returns {@code true} if no filter policy is set.
   405	     * Returns {@code false} for malformed filter policies (fail closed).
   406	     * <p>
   407	     * Only {@code FilterPolicyScope=MessageAttributes} is supported. When scope is
   408	     * {@code MessageBody}, filtering is skipped and the message is delivered (to avoid
   409	     * incorrectly dropping messages for an unsupported scope).
   410	     * <p>
   411	     * All keys in the policy must match (AND logic). Within each key's rule array,
   412	     * any matching element is sufficient (OR logic).
   413	     */
   414	    private boolean matchesFilterPolicy(Subscription sub, Map<String, String> messageAttributes) {
   415	        String filterPolicyJson = sub.getAttributes().get("FilterPolicy");
   416	        if (filterPolicyJson == null || filterPolicyJson.isBlank()) {
   417	            return true;
   418	        }
   419	        String scope = sub.getAttributes().getOrDefault("FilterPolicyScope", "MessageAttributes");
   420	        if ("MessageBody".equals(scope)) {
   421	            return true;
   422	        }
   423	        try {
   424	            JsonNode filterPolicy = objectMapper.readTree(filterPolicyJson);
   425	            if (!filterPolicy.isObject()) {
   426	                LOG.warnv("Invalid FilterPolicy (not a JSON object) for {0}", sub.getSubscriptionArn());
   427	                return false;
   428	            }
   429	            Map<String, String> attrs = messageAttributes != null ? messageAttributes : Map.of();
   430	            var fields = filterPolicy.fields();
   431	            while (fields.hasNext()) {
   432	                var entry = fields.next();
   433	                String key = entry.getKey();
   434	                JsonNode rules = entry.getValue();
   435	                String actualValue = attrs.get(key);
   436	                if (!matchesAttributeRules(actualValue, rules)) {
   437	                    return false;
   438	                }
   439	            }
   440	            return true;
   441	        } catch (Exception e) {
   442	            LOG.warnv("Failed to parse filter policy for {0}: {1}", sub.getSubscriptionArn(), e.getMessage());
   443	            return false;
   444	        }
   445	    }
   446	
   447	    /**
   448	     * Checks if an attribute value matches a single filter policy rule set.
   449	     * Rules must be a JSON array where ANY element matching means the rule passes (OR logic).
   450	     * Non-array rules are treated as non-matching.
   451	     */
   452	    private boolean matchesAttributeRules(String actualValue, JsonNode rules) {
   453	        if (!rules.isArray()) {
   454	            return false;
   455	        }
   456	        for (JsonNode rule : rules) {
   457	            if (rule.isTextual() && rule.asText().equals(actualValue)) {
   458	                return true;
   459	            }
   460	            if (rule.isNumber() && actualValue != null) {
   461	                try {
   462	                    if (new BigDecimal(actualValue).compareTo(rule.decimalValue()) == 0) {
   463	                        return true;
   464	                    }
   465	                } catch (NumberFormatException ignored) {
   466	                }
   467	            }
   468	            if (rule.isObject() && matchesObjectRule(rule, actualValue)) {
   469	                return true;
   470	            }
   471	        }
   472	        return false;
   473	    }
   474	
   475	    /**
   476	     * Evaluates a single object-type filter rule (exists, prefix, anything-but, numeric)
   477	     * against the actual attribute value.
   478	     */
   479	    private boolean matchesObjectRule(JsonNode rule, String actualValue) {
   480	        if (rule.has("exists")) {
   481	            boolean shouldExist = rule.get("exists").asBoolean();
   482	            return shouldExist ? actualValue != null : actualValue == null;
   483	        }
   484	        if (rule.has("prefix") && actualValue != null) {
   485	            return actualValue.startsWith(rule.get("prefix").asText());
   486	        }
   487	        if (rule.has("anything-but") && actualValue != null) {
   488	            return !containsValue(rule.get("anything-but"), actualValue);
   489	        }
   490	        if (rule.has("numeric") && actualValue != null) {
   491	            try {
   492	                return evaluateNumericCondition(new BigDecimal(actualValue), rule.get("numeric"));
   493	            } catch (NumberFormatException ignored) {
   494	            }
   495	        }
   496	        return false;
   497	    }
   498	
   499	    private boolean containsValue(JsonNode node, String value) {
   500	        if (node.isArray()) {
   501	            for (JsonNode element : node) {
   502	                if (element.asText().equals(value)) return true;
   503	            }
   504	            return false;
   505	        }
   506	        LOG.warnv("FilterPolicy 'anything-but' expected an array but got a scalar; treating as single-value list");
   507	        return node.asText().equals(value);
   508	    }
   509	
   510	    /**
   511	     * Evaluates a numeric condition array against a value.
   512	     * The conditions array contains alternating operator-target pairs (e.g. [">=", 100, "<", 200]).
   513	     * All pairs must match for the condition to pass (AND logic).
   514	     */
   515	    private boolean evaluateNumericCondition(BigDecimal value, JsonNode conditions) {
   516	        if (!conditions.isArray() || conditions.size() % 2 != 0) {
   517	            return false;
   518	        }
   519	        for (int i = 0; i < conditions.size(); i += 2) {
   520	            String op = conditions.get(i).asText();
   521	            BigDecimal target = conditions.get(i + 1).decimalValue();
   522	            int cmp = value.compareTo(target);
   523	            boolean matches = switch (op) {
   524	                case "=" -> cmp == 0;
   525	                case ">" -> cmp > 0;
   526	                case ">=" -> cmp >= 0;
   527	                case "<" -> cmp < 0;
   528	                case "<=" -> cmp <= 0;
   529	                default -> false;
   530	            };
   531	            if (!matches) return false;
   532	        }
   533	        return true;
   534	    }
   535	
   536	    private boolean isDuplicate(String topicArn, String deduplicationId) {
   537	        String cacheKey = topicArn + ":" + deduplicationId;
   538	        Instant now = Instant.now();
   539	        Instant existing = fifoDeduplicationCache.get(cacheKey);
   540	        if (existing != null && existing.plus(FIFO_DEDUP_WINDOW).isAfter(now)) {
   541	            return true;
   542	        }
   543	        fifoDeduplicationCache.put(cacheKey, now);
   544	        fifoDeduplicationCache.entrySet().removeIf(e -> e.getValue().plus(FIFO_DEDUP_WINDOW).isBefore(now));
   545	        return false;
   546	    }
   547	
   548	    private List<Subscription> subscriptionsByTopic(String topicArn, String region) {
   549	        List<Subscription> result = new ArrayList<>();
   550	        String prefix = "sub::" + region + "::";
   551	        for (String k : subscriptionStore.keys()) {
   552	            if (k.startsWith(prefix)) {
   553	                subscriptionStore.get(k).ifPresent(sub -> {
   554	                    if (topicArn.equals(sub.getTopicArn())) result.add(sub);
   555	                });
   556	            }
   557	        }
   558	        return result;
   559	    }
   560	
   561	    private void deliverMessage(Subscription sub, String message, String subject,
   562	                                Map<String, String> messageAttributes, String messageId,
   563	                                String topicArn, String messageGroupId) {
   564	        try {
   565	            switch (sub.getProtocol()) {
   566	                case "sqs" -> {
   567	                    String region = extractRegionFromArn(sub.getEndpoint());
   568	                    if (region == null) {
   569	                        region = extractRegionFromArn(topicArn);
   570	                    }
   571	                    String queueUrl = sqsArnToUrl(sub.getEndpoint());
   572	                    String envelope = buildSnsEnvelope(message, subject, messageAttributes, topicArn, messageId);
   573	                    sqsService.sendMessage(queueUrl, envelope, 0, messageGroupId, null, region);
   574	                    LOG.debugv("Delivered SNS message to SQS: {0} ({1}) in {2}",
   575	                            sub.getEndpoint(), queueUrl, region);
   576	                }
   577	                case "lambda" -> {
   578	                    String fnName = extractFunctionName(sub.getEndpoint());
   579	                    String region = extractRegionFromArn(sub.getEndpoint());
   580	                    String eventJson = buildSnsLambdaEvent(topicArn, messageId, message,
   581	                            subject, messageAttributes, sub.getSubscriptionArn());
   582	                    lambdaService.invoke(region, fnName, eventJson.getBytes(), InvocationType.Event);
   583	                    LOG.debugv("Delivered SNS message to Lambda: {0}", sub.getEndpoint());
   584	                }
   585	                case "email", "email-json" ->
   586	                    LOG.infov("SNS email delivery (stub): to={0}, subject={1}, message={2}",
   587	                            sub.getEndpoint(), subject, message);
   588	                case "sms" ->
   589	                    LOG.infov("SNS SMS delivery (stub): to={0}, message={1}", sub.getEndpoint(), message);
   590	                default -> LOG.debugv("Protocol {0} delivery not implemented, skipping: {1}",
   591	                        sub.getProtocol(), sub.getEndpoint());
   592	            }
   593	        } catch (Exception e) {
   594	            LOG.warnv("Failed to deliver SNS message to {0}: {1}", sub.getEndpoint(), e.getMessage());
   595	        }
   596	    }
   597	
   598	    private String buildSnsLambdaEvent(String topicArn, String messageId, String message,
   599	                                       String subject, Map<String, String> messageAttributes,
   600	                                       String subscriptionArn) {
   601	        try {
   602	            String timestamp = DateTimeFormatter.ISO_INSTANT.format(Instant.now());
   603	            ObjectNode snsNode = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   604	            snsNode.put("Type", "Notification");
   605	            snsNode.put("MessageId", messageId);
   606	            snsNode.put("TopicArn", topicArn);
   607	            if (subject != null) {
   608	                snsNode.put("Subject", subject);
   609	            } else {
   610	                snsNode.putNull("Subject");
   611	            }
   612	            snsNode.put("Message", message);
   613	            snsNode.put("Timestamp", timestamp);
   614	            snsNode.put("SignatureVersion", "1");
   615	            snsNode.put("Signature", "EXAMPLE");
   616	            snsNode.put("SigningCertUrl", "EXAMPLE");
   617	            snsNode.put("UnsubscribeUrl", "EXAMPLE");
   618	            ObjectNode attrs = snsNode.putObject("MessageAttributes");
   619	            if (messageAttributes != null) {
   620	                for (var entry : messageAttributes.entrySet()) {
   621	                    ObjectNode attr = attrs.putObject(entry.getKey());
   622	                    attr.put("Type", "String");
   623	                    attr.put("Value", entry.getValue());
   624	                }
   625	            }
   626	            ObjectNode record = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   627	            record.put("EventVersion", "1.0");
   628	            record.put("EventSubscriptionArn", subscriptionArn);
   629	            record.put("EventSource", "aws:sns");
   630	            record.set("Sns", snsNode);
   631	            ObjectNode root = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   632	            root.putArray("Records").add(record);
   633	            return objectMapper.writeValueAsString(root);
   634	        } catch (Exception e) {
   635	            return "{\"Records\":[]}";
   636	        }
   637	    }

   683	    private static String sha256(String message) {
   684	        try {
   685	            MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
   686	            byte[] hash = md.digest(message.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   687	            var sb = new StringBuilder();
   688	            for (byte b : hash) {
   689	                sb.append(String.format("%02x", b));
   690	            }
   691	            return sb.toString();
   692	        } catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException e) {
   693	            return UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   694	        }
   695	    }

    private void loadPersistedMessages() {
        if (messageStore == null) {
            return;
        }
        for (String key : messageStore.keys()) {
            messageStore.get(key).ifPresent(msgs ->
                    messagesByQueue.put(key, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>(msgs)));
        }
    }

    private void loadPersistedDedup() {
        if (dedupStore == null) {
            return;
        }
        Instant now = Instant.now();
        for (String key : dedupStore.keys()) {
            dedupStore.get(key).ifPresent(entries -> {
                ConcurrentHashMap<String, Instant> active = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
                entries.forEach((dedupId, expiryMs) -> {
                    Instant expiry = Instant.ofEpochMilli(expiryMs);
                    if (now.isBefore(expiry)) {
                        active.put(dedupId, expiry);
                    }
                });
                if (!active.isEmpty()) {
                    deduplicationCache.put(key, active);
                }
            });
        }
    }

    private void persistMessages(String storageKey) {
        if (messageStore == null) {
            return;
        }

        var messages = messagesByQueue.get(storageKey);
        if (messages != null) {
            // Weakly-consistent snapshot; messages modified concurrently may or may not appear.
            messageStore.put(storageKey, new ArrayList<>(messages));
        } else {
            messageStore.delete(storageKey);
        }
    }

    private void persistDedup(String storageKey) {
        if (dedupStore == null) {
            return;
        }
        var dedupMap = deduplicationCache.get(storageKey);
        if (dedupMap != null && !dedupMap.isEmpty()) {
            Map<String, Long> serializable = new HashMap<>();
            dedupMap.forEach((id, expiry) -> serializable.put(id, expiry.toEpochMilli()));
            dedupStore.put(storageKey, serializable);
        } else {
            dedupStore.delete(storageKey);
        }
    }

        return createQueue(queueName, attributes, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());

   318	
   319	    public Message sendMessage(String queueUrl, String body, int delaySeconds,
   320	                               String messageGroupId, String messageDeduplicationId,
   321	                               Map<String, MessageAttributeValue> messageAttributes,
   322	                               String region) {
   323	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, queueUrl);
   324	        Queue queue = queueStore.get(storageKey)
   325	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("AWS.SimpleQueueService.NonExistentQueue",
   326	                        "The specified queue does not exist.", 400));
   327	
   328	        if (body.length() > maxMessageSize) {
   329	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValue",
   330	                    "Message body must be shorter than " + maxMessageSize + " bytes.", 400);
   331	        }
   332	
   333	        // FIFO queue validation
   334	        if (queue.isFifo()) {
   335	            if (messageGroupId == null || messageGroupId.isEmpty()) {
   336	                throw new AwsException("MissingParameter",
   337	                        "The request must contain the parameter MessageGroupId.", 400);
   338	            }
   339	            // Resolve deduplication ID
   340	            String dedupId = messageDeduplicationId;
   341	            if (dedupId == null || dedupId.isEmpty()) {
   342	                if ("true" .equalsIgnoreCase(queue.getAttributes().get("ContentBasedDeduplication"))) {
   343	                    dedupId = computeMd5(body);
   344	                } else {
   345	                    throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValue",
   346	                            "The queue should either have ContentBasedDeduplication enabled or " +
   347	                                    "MessageDeduplicationId provided.", 400);
   348	                }
   349	            }
   350	
   351	            // Check deduplication window — atomic putIfAbsent to avoid race condition
   352	            cleanupDeduplicationCache(storageKey);
   353	            var dedupMap = deduplicationCache.computeIfAbsent(storageKey, k -> new ConcurrentHashMap<>());
   354	            Instant expiry = Instant.now().plusSeconds(DEDUP_WINDOW_SECONDS);
   355	            Instant previous = dedupMap.putIfAbsent(dedupId, expiry);
   356	            persistDedup(storageKey);
   357	            if (previous != null && Instant.now().isBefore(previous)) {
   358	                // Duplicate within window — return the original message idempotently
   359	                var messages = messagesByQueue.getOrDefault(storageKey, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
   360	                for (Message msg : messages) {
   361	                    if (dedupId.equals(msg.getMessageDeduplicationId())) {
   362	                        return msg;
   363	                    }
   364	                }
   365	            }
   366	
   367	            Message message = new Message(body);
   368	            message.setMessageGroupId(messageGroupId);
   369	            message.setMessageDeduplicationId(dedupId);
   370	            message.setSequenceNumber(sequenceCounter.incrementAndGet());
   371	            if (messageAttributes != null && !messageAttributes.isEmpty()) {
   372	                message.getMessageAttributes().putAll(messageAttributes);
   373	                message.updateMd5OfMessageAttributes();
   374	            }
   375	
   376	            messagesByQueue.computeIfAbsent(storageKey, k -> new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>()).add(message);
   377	            persistMessages(storageKey);
   378	            notifyReceivers(storageKey);
   379	            LOG.debugv("Sent FIFO message {0} to queue {1}, group={2}, seq={3}",
   380	                    message.getMessageId(), queueUrl, messageGroupId, message.getSequenceNumber());

   401	    private void notifyReceivers(String storageKey) {
   402	        Object lock = queueLocks.get(storageKey);
   403	        if (lock != null) {
   404	            synchronized (lock) {
   405	                lock.notifyAll();
   406	            }
   407	        }
   408	    }
   409	
   410	    private void cleanupDeduplicationCache(String queueUrl) {
   411	        var dedupMap = deduplicationCache.get(queueUrl);
   412	        if (dedupMap != null) {
   413	            Instant now = Instant.now();
   414	            dedupMap.entrySet().removeIf(e -> now.isAfter(e.getValue()));
   415	        }
   416	    }
   417	
   418	    private static String computeMd5(String input) {
   419	        try {
   420	            var md = java.security.MessageDigest.getInstance("MD5");
   421	            byte[] digest = md.digest(input.getBytes(java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   422	            var sb = new StringBuilder();
   423	            for (byte b : digest) {
   424	                sb.append(String.format("%02x", b));
   425	            }
   426	            return sb.toString();
   427	        } catch (java.security.NoSuchAlgorithmException e) {
   428	            return "";
   429	        }
   430	    }

/testbed/src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/core/storage/StorageFactory.java
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.config.EmulatorConfig;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
import jakarta.inject.Inject;
import org.jboss.logging.Logger;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

/**
 * Factory that creates StorageBackend instances based on configuration.
 * Tracks all created backends for lifecycle management.
 */
@ApplicationScoped
public class StorageFactory {

    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(StorageFactory.class);

    private final EmulatorConfig config;
    private final List<StorageBackend<?, ?>> allBackends = new ArrayList<>();
    private final List<HybridStorage<?, ?>> hybridBackends = new ArrayList<>();
    private final List<WalStorage<?, ?>> walBackends = new ArrayList<>();

    @Inject
    public StorageFactory(EmulatorConfig config) {
        this.config = config;
    }

    /**
     * Create a storage backend for the given service.
     *
     * @param serviceName   the service name (ssm, sqs, s3)
     * @param fileName      the JSON file name for persistent storage
     * @param typeReference Jackson type reference for deserialization
     */
    public <K, V> StorageBackend<K, V> create(String serviceName, String fileName,
                                               TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference) {
        String mode = resolveMode(serviceName);
        long flushInterval = resolveFlushInterval(serviceName);
        Path basePath = Path.of(config.storage().persistentPath());
        Path filePath = basePath.resolve(fileName);

        LOG.infov("Creating {0} storage for service {1} (file: {2})", mode, serviceName, filePath);

        StorageBackend<K, V> backend = switch (mode) {
            case "memory" -> new InMemoryStorage<>();
            case "persistent" -> new PersistentStorage<>(filePath, typeReference);
            case "hybrid" -> {
                var hybrid = new HybridStorage<>(filePath, typeReference, flushInterval);
                hybridBackends.add(hybrid);
                yield hybrid;
            }
            case "wal" -> {
                Path snapshotPath = basePath.resolve(fileName.replace(".json", "-snapshot.json"));
                Path walFilePath = basePath.resolve(fileName.replace(".json", ".wal"));
                long compactionInterval = config.storage().wal().compactionIntervalMs();
                var wal = new WalStorage<>(snapshotPath, walFilePath, typeReference, compactionInterval);
                walBackends.add(wal);
                yield wal;
            }
            default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unknown storage mode: " + mode);
        };

        // load because loadAll() may run before the service is initialized
        backend.load();

        allBackends.add(backend);
        return backend;
    }

    /** Load all storage backends from disk. */
    public void loadAll() {
        for (StorageBackend<?, ?> backend : allBackends) {
            backend.load();
        }
    }

    /** Flush all storage backends to disk. */
    public void flushAll() {
        for (StorageBackend<?, ?> backend : allBackends) {
            backend.flush();
        }
    }

    /** Shutdown all managed backends (stop schedulers, close connections). */
    public void shutdownAll() {
        for (HybridStorage<?, ?> hybrid : hybridBackends) {
            hybrid.shutdown();
        }
        for (WalStorage<?, ?> wal : walBackends) {
            wal.shutdown();
        }
        flushAll();
    }

    private String resolveMode(String serviceName) {
        String globalMode = config.storage().mode();
        return switch (serviceName) {
            case "ssm" -> config.storage().services().ssm().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "sqs" -> config.storage().services().sqs().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "s3" -> config.storage().services().s3().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "dynamodb" -> config.storage().services().dynamodb().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "sns" -> config.storage().services().sns().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "lambda" -> config.storage().services().lambda().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "cloudwatchlogs" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchlogs().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "cloudwatchmetrics" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchmetrics().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "secretsmanager" -> config.storage().services().secretsmanager().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            case "opensearch" -> config.storage().services().opensearch().mode().orElse(globalMode);
            default -> globalMode;
        };
    }

    private long resolveFlushInterval(String serviceName) {
        return switch (serviceName) {
            case "ssm" -> config.storage().services().ssm().flushIntervalMs();
            case "dynamodb" -> config.storage().services().dynamodb().flushIntervalMs();
/testbed/src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/core/storage/InMemoryStorage.java
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.function.Predicate;

/**
 * Thread-safe in-memory storage backed by ConcurrentHashMap.
 * No persistence — data is lost on shutdown unless explicitly flushed.
 */
public class InMemoryStorage<K, V> implements StorageBackend<K, V> {

    private final ConcurrentHashMap<K, V> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

    @Override
    public void put(K key, V value) {
        store.put(key, value);
    }

    @Override
    public Optional<V> get(K key) {
        return Optional.ofNullable(store.get(key));
    }

    @Override
    public void delete(K key) {
        store.remove(key);
    }

    @Override
    public List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter) {
        List<V> result = new ArrayList<>();
        store.forEach((k, v) -> {
            if (keyFilter.test(k)) {
                result.add(v);
            }
        });
        return result;
    }

    @Override
    public Set<K> keys() {
        return Collections.unmodifiableSet(store.keySet());
    }

    @Override
    public void flush() {
        // No-op for in-memory storage
    }

    @Override
    public void load() {
        // No-op for in-memory storage
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
        store.clear();
    }
}

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import org.jboss.logging.Logger;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.nio.file.StandardCopyOption;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import java.util.function.Predicate;

/**
 * Hybrid storage: in-memory reads with async flush to disk.
 * Writes go to memory immediately, then flushed to disk periodically.
 */
public class HybridStorage<K, V> implements StorageBackend<K, V> {

    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(HybridStorage.class);

    private final ConcurrentHashMap<K, V> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private final Path filePath;
    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    private final TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference;
    private final ScheduledExecutorService scheduler;
    private final AtomicBoolean dirty = new AtomicBoolean(false);

    public HybridStorage(Path filePath, TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference, long flushIntervalMs) {
        this.filePath = filePath;
        this.typeReference = typeReference;
        this.objectMapper = new ObjectMapper();
        this.objectMapper.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
        this.objectMapper.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
        this.objectMapper.enable(SerializationFeature.INDENT_OUTPUT);

        this.scheduler = Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(r -> {
            Thread t = new Thread(r, "hybrid-storage-flush");
            t.setDaemon(true);
            return t;
        });
        this.scheduler.scheduleAtFixedRate(this::flushIfDirty, flushIntervalMs, flushIntervalMs, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
    }

    @Override
    public void put(K key, V value) {
        store.put(key, value);
        dirty.set(true);
    }

    @Override
    public Optional<V> get(K key) {
        return Optional.ofNullable(store.get(key));
    }

    @Override
    public void delete(K key) {
        store.remove(key);
        dirty.set(true);
    }

    @Override
    public List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter) {
        return store.entrySet().stream()
                .filter(e -> keyFilter.test(e.getKey()))
                .map(Map.Entry::getValue)
                .toList();
    }

    @Override
    public Set<K> keys() {
        return Collections.unmodifiableSet(store.keySet());
    }

    @Override
    public void flush() {
        persistToDisk();
    }

    @Override
    public void load() {
        if (!Files.exists(filePath)) {
            LOG.debugv("No persistent file found at {0}, starting with empty store", filePath);
            return;
        }
        try {
            Map<K, V> data = objectMapper.readValue(filePath.toFile(), typeReference);
            store.clear();
            store.putAll(data);
            LOG.infov("Loaded {0} entries from {1}", store.size(), filePath);
        } catch (IOException e) {
            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to load data from {0}", filePath);
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
        store.clear();
        dirty.set(true);
    }

    public void shutdown() {
        scheduler.shutdown();
        try {
            if (!scheduler.awaitTermination(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS)) {
                scheduler.shutdownNow();
            }
        } catch (InterruptedException e) {
            scheduler.shutdownNow();
/testbed/src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/core/storage/PersistentStorage.java
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import org.jboss.logging.Logger;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.nio.file.StandardCopyOption;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.function.Predicate;

/**
 * JSON file-backed persistent storage.
 * Loads all data into memory on startup for fast reads.
 * Write-through on every put/delete.
 * Uses atomic writes (temp file + rename) for safety.
 */
public class PersistentStorage<K, V> implements StorageBackend<K, V> {

    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(PersistentStorage.class);

    private final ConcurrentHashMap<K, V> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private final Path filePath;
    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    private final TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference;

    public PersistentStorage(Path filePath, TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference) {
        this.filePath = filePath;
        this.typeReference = typeReference;
        this.objectMapper = new ObjectMapper();
        this.objectMapper.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
        this.objectMapper.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
        this.objectMapper.enable(SerializationFeature.INDENT_OUTPUT);
    }

    @Override
    public void put(K key, V value) {
        store.put(key, value);
        persistToDisk();
    }

    @Override
    public Optional<V> get(K key) {
        return Optional.ofNullable(store.get(key));
    }

    @Override
    public void delete(K key) {
        store.remove(key);
        persistToDisk();
    }

    @Override
    public List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter) {
        return store.entrySet().stream()
                .filter(e -> keyFilter.test(e.getKey()))
                .map(Map.Entry::getValue)
                .toList();
    }

    @Override
    public Set<K> keys() {
        return Collections.unmodifiableSet(store.keySet());
    }

    @Override
    public void flush() {
        persistToDisk();
    }

    @Override
    public void load() {
        if (!Files.exists(filePath)) {
            LOG.debugv("No persistent file found at {0}, starting with empty store", filePath);
            return;
        }
        try {
            Map<K, V> data = objectMapper.readValue(filePath.toFile(), typeReference);
            store.clear();
            store.putAll(data);
            LOG.infov("Loaded {0} entries from {1}", store.size(), filePath);
        } catch (IOException e) {
            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to load data from {0}", filePath);
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
        store.clear();
        persistToDisk();
    }

    private synchronized void persistToDisk() {
        try {
            Files.createDirectories(filePath.getParent());
            Path tempFile = filePath.resolveSibling(filePath.getFileName() + ".tmp");
            objectMapper.writeValue(tempFile.toFile(), store);
            Files.move(tempFile, filePath, StandardCopyOption.REPLACE_EXISTING, StandardCopyOption.ATOMIC_MOVE);
        } catch (IOException e) {
            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to persist data to {0}", filePath);
        }
    }
}
/testbed/src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/core/storage/StorageBackend.java
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Predicate;

/**
 * Generic storage abstraction for AWS emulator services.
 *
 * @param <K> the key type
 * @param <V> the value type
 */
public interface StorageBackend<K, V> {

    void put(K key, V value);

    Optional<V> get(K key);

    void delete(K key);

    List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter);

    /** Return all keys in this store. */
    Set<K> keys();

    /** Persist data to disk if applicable. */
    void flush();

    /** Load data from disk on startup. */
    void load();

    /** Clear all data. */
    void clear();
}

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.dataformat.cbor.CBORFactory;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import org.jboss.logging.Logger;

import java.io.*;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.nio.file.StandardCopyOption;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.*;
import java.util.concurrent.locks.ReentrantReadWriteLock;
import java.util.function.Predicate;

/**
 * Write-Ahead Log storage: in-memory reads with append-only binary WAL for durability.
 * Periodic compaction writes a full snapshot and truncates the WAL.
 * On startup: load snapshot, then replay WAL entries after snapshot.
 *
 * Binary WAL entry format:
 *   PUT:    [0x01] [4-byte key length] [key bytes] [4-byte value length] [value bytes]
 *   DELETE: [0x02] [4-byte key length] [key bytes]
 *
 * Key and value bytes are serialized via Jackson CBOR (compact binary format).
 * Snapshot files use indented JSON for debuggability.
 */
public class WalStorage<K, V> implements StorageBackend<K, V> {

    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(WalStorage.class);

    static final byte OP_PUT = 0x01;
    static final byte OP_DELETE = 0x02;

    private final ConcurrentHashMap<K, V> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private final Path snapshotPath;

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.config.EmulatorConfig;
import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
import jakarta.inject.Inject;
import jakarta.ws.rs.core.HttpHeaders;

import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

@ApplicationScoped
public class RegionResolver {

    // Matches: Credential=AKID/20260215/us-west-2/s3/aws4_request
    private static final Pattern CREDENTIAL_REGION_PATTERN =
            Pattern.compile("Credential=\\S+/\\d{8}/([^/]+)/");

    private final String defaultRegion;
    private final String defaultAccountId;

    @Inject
    public RegionResolver(EmulatorConfig config) {
        this(config.defaultRegion(), config.defaultAccountId());
    }

    public RegionResolver(String defaultRegion, String defaultAccountId) {
        this.defaultRegion = defaultRegion;
        this.defaultAccountId = defaultAccountId;
    }

    public String resolveRegion(HttpHeaders headers) {
        if (headers == null) {
            return defaultRegion;
        }
        String auth = headers.getHeaderString("Authorization");
        if (auth == null || auth.isEmpty()) {
            return defaultRegion;
        }
        Matcher matcher = CREDENTIAL_REGION_PATTERN.matcher(auth);
        if (matcher.find()) {
            return matcher.group(1);
        }
        return defaultRegion;
    }

    public String getDefaultRegion() {
        return defaultRegion;
    }

    public String getAccountId() {
        return defaultAccountId;
    }

    public String buildArn(String service, String region, String resource) {
        return "arn:aws:" + service + ":" + region + ":" + defaultAccountId + ":" + resource;
    }
}
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonIgnoreProperties;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import io.quarkus.runtime.annotations.RegisterForReflection;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

@RegisterForReflection
@JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
public class Subscription {

    @JsonProperty("SubscriptionArn")
    private String subscriptionArn;

    @JsonProperty("TopicArn")
    private String topicArn;

    @JsonProperty("Protocol")
    private String protocol;

    @JsonProperty("Endpoint")
    private String endpoint;

    @JsonProperty("Owner")
    private String owner;

    @JsonProperty("Attributes")
    private Map<String, String> attributes = new HashMap<>();

    public Subscription() {}

    public Subscription(String subscriptionArn, String topicArn, String protocol, String endpoint, String owner) {
        this.subscriptionArn = subscriptionArn;
        this.topicArn = topicArn;
        this.protocol = protocol;
        this.endpoint = endpoint;
        this.owner = owner;
    }

    public String getSubscriptionArn() { return subscriptionArn; }
    public void setSubscriptionArn(String subscriptionArn) { this.subscriptionArn = subscriptionArn; }

    public String getTopicArn() { return topicArn; }
    public void setTopicArn(String topicArn) { this.topicArn = topicArn; }

    public String getProtocol() { return protocol; }
    public void setProtocol(String protocol) { this.protocol = protocol; }

    public String getEndpoint() { return endpoint; }
    public void setEndpoint(String endpoint) { this.endpoint = endpoint; }

    public String getOwner() { return owner; }
    public void setOwner(String owner) { this.owner = owner; }

    public Map<String, String> getAttributes() { return attributes; }
    public void setAttributes(Map<String, String> attributes) { this.attributes = attributes; }
}
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonIgnoreProperties;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import io.quarkus.runtime.annotations.RegisterForReflection;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

@RegisterForReflection
@JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
public class Topic {

    @JsonProperty("Name")
    private String name;

    @JsonProperty("TopicArn")
    private String topicArn;

    @JsonProperty("Attributes")
    private Map<String, String> attributes = new HashMap<>();

    @JsonProperty("Tags")
    private Map<String, String> tags = new HashMap<>();

    @JsonProperty("CreatedAt")
    private Instant createdAt;

    public Topic() {}

    public Topic(String name, String topicArn) {
        this.name = name;
        this.topicArn = topicArn;
        this.createdAt = Instant.now();
        this.attributes.put("TopicArn", topicArn);
        this.attributes.put("DisplayName", "");
        this.attributes.put("Policy", "");
        this.attributes.put("DeliveryPolicy", "");
        this.attributes.put("EffectiveDeliveryPolicy", "");
    }

    public String getName() { return name; }
    public void setName(String name) { this.name = name; }

    public String getTopicArn() { return topicArn; }
    public void setTopicArn(String topicArn) { this.topicArn = topicArn; }

    public Map<String, String> getAttributes() { return attributes; }
    public void setAttributes(Map<String, String> attributes) { this.attributes = attributes; }

    public Map<String, String> getTags() { return tags; }
    public void setTags(Map<String, String> tags) { this.tags = tags; }

    public Instant getCreatedAt() { return createdAt; }
    public void setCreatedAt(Instant createdAt) { this.createdAt = createdAt; }
}

                        }),

                        }),
                storageFactory.create("sqs", "sqs-dedup.json",
                        new TypeReference<Map<String, Map<String, Long>>>() {
                        }),

                config.services().sqs().maxMessageSize(),
                config.effectiveBaseUrl(),
                regionResolver
        );
    }

    /**
     * Package-private constructor for testing.
     */
    SqsService(StorageBackend<String, Queue> queueStore,
               int defaultVisibilityTimeout, int maxMessageSize, String baseUrl) {
        this(queueStore, null, null, defaultVisibilityTimeout, maxMessageSize, baseUrl,
                new RegionResolver("us-east-1", "000000000000"));
    }

    SqsService(StorageBackend<String, Queue> queueStore, StorageBackend<String, List<Message>> messageStore,
               StorageBackend<String, Map<String, Long>> dedupStore,
               int defaultVisibilityTimeout, int maxMessageSize, String baseUrl,
               RegionResolver regionResolver) {
        this.queueStore = queueStore;
        this.messageStore = messageStore;
        this.dedupStore = dedupStore;
        this.defaultVisibilityTimeout = defaultVisibilityTimeout;
        this.maxMessageSize = maxMessageSize;
        this.baseUrl = baseUrl;
        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
        loadPersistedMessages();
        loadPersistedDedup();
    }

    private void loadPersistedMessages() {
        if (messageStore == null) {
            return;
        }
        for (String key : messageStore.keys()) {
            messageStore.get(key).ifPresent(msgs ->
                    messagesByQueue.put(key, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>(msgs)));
        }
    }

        if (dedupStore == null) {
            return;

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.AwsErrorResponse;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model.Subscription;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model.Topic;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ArrayNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
import jakarta.inject.Inject;
import jakarta.ws.rs.core.Response;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;

/**
 * SNS JSON protocol handler (application/x-amz-json-1.0).
 * Called by AwsJsonController for SNS_20100331.* targeted requests.
 */
@ApplicationScoped
public class SnsJsonHandler {

    private final SnsService snsService;
    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;

    @Inject
    public SnsJsonHandler(SnsService snsService, ObjectMapper objectMapper) {
        this.snsService = snsService;
        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
    }

    public Response handle(String action, JsonNode request, String region) {
        return switch (action) {
            case "CreateTopic" -> handleCreateTopic(request, region);
            case "DeleteTopic" -> handleDeleteTopic(request, region);
            case "ListTopics" -> handleListTopics(request, region);
            case "GetTopicAttributes" -> handleGetTopicAttributes(request, region);
            case "SetTopicAttributes" -> handleSetTopicAttributes(request, region);
            case "Subscribe" -> handleSubscribe(request, region);
            case "Unsubscribe" -> handleUnsubscribe(request, region);
            case "ListSubscriptions" -> handleListSubscriptions(request, region);
            case "ListSubscriptionsByTopic" -> handleListSubscriptionsByTopic(request, region);
            case "Publish" -> handlePublish(request, region);
            case "PublishBatch" -> handlePublishBatch(request, region);
            case "GetSubscriptionAttributes" -> handleGetSubscriptionAttributes(request, region);
            case "SetSubscriptionAttributes" -> handleSetSubscriptionAttributes(request, region);
            case "ConfirmSubscription" -> handleConfirmSubscription(request, region);
            case "TagResource" -> handleTagResource(request, region);
            case "UntagResource" -> handleUntagResource(request, region);
            case "ListTagsForResource" -> handleListTagsForResource(request, region);
            default -> Response.status(400)
                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("UnsupportedOperation", "Operation " + action + " is not supported."))
                    .build();
        };
    }

    private Response handleCreateTopic(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
        Map<String, String> attributes = jsonNodeToMap(request.path("Attributes"));
        Map<String, String> tags = new HashMap<>();
        JsonNode tagsNode = request.path("Tags");
        if (tagsNode.isArray()) {
            for (JsonNode tag : tagsNode) {
                tags.put(tag.path("Key").asText(), tag.path("Value").asText());
            }
        }
        Topic topic = snsService.createTopic(name, attributes, tags, region);
        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
        response.put("TopicArn", topic.getTopicArn());
        return Response.ok(response).build();
    }

    private Response handleDeleteTopic(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String topicArn = request.path("TopicArn").asText(null);
        snsService.deleteTopic(topicArn, region);
        return Response.ok().build();
    }

    private Response handleListTopics(JsonNode request, String region) {
        List<Topic> topics = snsService.listTopics(region);
        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
        ArrayNode topicsArray = response.putArray("Topics");
        for (Topic t : topics) {
            ObjectNode entry = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
            entry.put("TopicArn", t.getTopicArn());
            topicsArray.add(entry);
        }
        return Response.ok(response).build();
    }

    private Response handleGetTopicAttributes(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String topicArn = request.path("TopicArn").asText(null);
        Map<String, String> attrs = snsService.getTopicAttributes(topicArn, region);
        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
        ObjectNode attrsNode = response.putObject("Attributes");
        for (var entry : attrs.entrySet()) {
            attrsNode.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
        }
        return Response.ok(response).build();
    }

    private Response handleSetTopicAttributes(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String topicArn = request.path("TopicArn").asText(null);
        String attributeName = request.path("AttributeName").asText(null);
        String attributeValue = request.path("AttributeValue").asText(null);
        snsService.setTopicAttributes(topicArn, attributeName, attributeValue, region);
        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
    }

    private Response handleSubscribe(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String topicArn = request.path("TopicArn").asText(null);
        String protocol = request.path("Protocol").asText(null);
        String endpoint = request.path("Endpoint").asText(null);
        Subscription sub = snsService.subscribe(topicArn, protocol, endpoint, region);
        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
        response.put("SubscriptionArn", sub.getSubscriptionArn());
        return Response.ok(response).build();
    }

    private Response handleUnsubscribe(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String subscriptionArn = request.path("SubscriptionArn").asText(null);
        snsService.unsubscribe(subscriptionArn, region);
        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
    }

    private Response handleListSubscriptions(JsonNode request, String region) {
        List<Subscription> subs = snsService.listSubscriptions(region);
        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
        ArrayNode items = response.putArray("Subscriptions");
        for (Subscription s : subs) {
            items.add(subscriptionToNode(s));
        }
        return Response.ok(response).build();
    }

    private Response handleListSubscriptionsByTopic(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String topicArn = request.path("TopicArn").asText(null);
        List<Subscription> subs = snsService.listSubscriptionsByTopic(topicArn, region);
        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
        ArrayNode subsArray = response.putArray("Subscriptions");
        for (Subscription s : subs) {
            subsArray.add(subscriptionToNode(s));
        }
        return Response.ok(response).build();
    }

    private Response handlePublish(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String topicArn = request.path("TopicArn").asText(null);
        String targetArn = request.path("TargetArn").asText(null);
        String phoneNumber = request.path("PhoneNumber").asText(null);
        String message = request.path("Message").asText(null);
        String subject = request.path("Subject").asText(null);

        Map<String, String> attributes = new HashMap<>();
        JsonNode attrsNode = request.path("MessageAttributes");
        if (attrsNode.isObject()) {
            attrsNode.fields().forEachRemaining(entry -> {
                attributes.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue().path("StringValue").asText());
            });
        }

        String messageId = snsService.publish(topicArn, targetArn, phoneNumber, message, subject, attributes, region);
        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
        response.put("MessageId", messageId);
        return Response.ok(response).build();
    }

    private Response handleTagResource(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String resourceArn = request.path("ResourceArn").asText(null);
        Map<String, String> tags = new HashMap<>();
        JsonNode tagsNode = request.path("Tags");
        if (tagsNode.isArray()) {
            for (JsonNode tag : tagsNode) {
                tags.put(tag.path("Key").asText(), tag.path("Value").asText());
            }
        }
        snsService.tagResource(resourceArn, tags, region);
        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
    }

    private Response handleUntagResource(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String resourceArn = request.path("ResourceArn").asText(null);
        List<String> tagKeys = new ArrayList<>();
        JsonNode keysNode = request.path("TagKeys");
        if (keysNode.isArray()) {
            for (JsonNode key : keysNode) {
                tagKeys.add(key.asText());
            }
        }
        snsService.untagResource(resourceArn, tagKeys, region);
        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
    }

    private Response handleListTagsForResource(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String resourceArn = request.path("ResourceArn").asText(null);
        Map<String, String> tags = snsService.listTagsForResource(resourceArn, region);
        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
        ArrayNode tagsArray = response.putArray("Tags");
        for (var entry : tags.entrySet()) {
            ObjectNode tag = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
            tag.put("Key", entry.getKey());
            tag.put("Value", entry.getValue());
            tagsArray.add(tag);
        }
        return Response.ok(response).build();
    }

    private Response handlePublishBatch(JsonNode request, String region) {
        String topicArn = request.path("TopicArn").asText(null);
        List<Map<String, Object>> entries = new ArrayList<>();

                entry.put("Message", entryNode.path("Message").asText(null));
                entry.put("Subject", entryNode.path("Subject").asText(null));
                entry.put("MessageGroupId", entryNode.path("MessageGroupId").asText(null));
                entry.put("MessageDeduplicationId", entryNode.path("MessageDeduplicationId").asText(null));

                JsonNode attrsNode = entryNode.path("MessageAttributes");
                if (attrsNode.isObject()) {

                        messageAttributes.put(field.getKey(), field.getValue().path("StringValue").asText())
                    );
                    entry.put("MessageAttributes", messageAttributes);
                }

                entries.add(entry);
            }
        }
