package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.*;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model.Subscription;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model.Topic;
import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
import jakarta.inject.Inject;
import jakarta.ws.rs.core.MultivaluedMap;
import jakarta.ws.rs.core.Response;
import org.jboss.logging.Logger;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

/**
 * Query-protocol handler for SNS actions.
 * Receives pre-dispatched calls from {@link AwsQueryController}.
 */
@ApplicationScoped
public class SnsQueryHandler {

    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(SnsQueryHandler.class);

    private final SnsService snsService;

    @Inject
    public SnsQueryHandler(SnsService snsService) {
        this.snsService = snsService;
    }

    public Response handle(String action, MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        LOG.debugv("SNS action: {0}", action);

        return switch (action) {
            case "CreateTopic" -> handleCreateTopic(params, region);
            case "DeleteTopic" -> handleDeleteTopic(params, region);
            case "ListTopics" -> handleListTopics(params, region);
            case "GetTopicAttributes" -> handleGetTopicAttributes(params, region);
            case "SetTopicAttributes" -> handleSetTopicAttributes(params, region);
            case "Subscribe" -> handleSubscribe(params, region);
            case "Unsubscribe" -> handleUnsubscribe(params, region);
            case "ListSubscriptions" -> handleListSubscriptions(params, region);
            case "ListSubscriptionsByTopic" -> handleListSubscriptionsByTopic(params, region);
            case "Publish" -> handlePublish(params, region);
            case "PublishBatch" -> handlePublishBatch(params, region);
            case "GetSubscriptionAttributes" -> handleGetSubscriptionAttributes(params, region);
            case "SetSubscriptionAttributes" -> handleSetSubscriptionAttributes(params, region);
            case "ConfirmSubscription" -> handleConfirmSubscription(params, region);
            case "TagResource" -> handleTagResource(params, region);
            case "UntagResource" -> handleUntagResource(params, region);
            case "ListTagsForResource" -> handleListTagsForResource(params, region);
            default -> AwsQueryResponse.error("UnsupportedOperation",
                    "Operation " + action + " is not supported by SNS.", AwsNamespaces.SNS, 400);
        };
    }

    private Response handleCreateTopic(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String name = getParam(params, "Name");
        Map<String, String> attributes = extractSnsAttributes(params, "Attributes");
        Map<String, String> tags = extractSnsTags(params);
        Topic topic = snsService.createTopic(name, attributes, tags, region);

        String result = new XmlBuilder().elem("TopicArn", topic.getTopicArn()).build();
        return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("CreateTopic", AwsNamespaces.SNS, result)).build();
    }

    private Response handleDeleteTopic(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String topicArn = getParam(params, "TopicArn");
        try {
            snsService.deleteTopic(topicArn, region);
            return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelopeNoResult("DeleteTopic", AwsNamespaces.SNS)).build();
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            return xmlErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage(), e.getHttpStatus());
        }
    }

    private Response handleListTopics(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        List<Topic> topics = snsService.listTopics(region);

        var xml = new XmlBuilder().start("Topics");
        for (Topic t : topics) {
            xml.start("member").elem("TopicArn", t.getTopicArn()).end("member");
        }
        xml.end("Topics");
        return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("ListTopics", AwsNamespaces.SNS, xml.build())).build();
    }

    private Response handleGetTopicAttributes(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String topicArn = getParam(params, "TopicArn");
        try {
            Map<String, String> attrs = snsService.getTopicAttributes(topicArn, region);

            var xml = new XmlBuilder().start("Attributes");
            for (var entry : attrs.entrySet()) {
                xml.start("entry")
                   .elem("key", entry.getKey())
                   .elem("value", entry.getValue())
                   .end("entry");
            }
            xml.end("Attributes");
            return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("GetTopicAttributes", AwsNamespaces.SNS, xml.build())).build();
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            return xmlErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage(), e.getHttpStatus());
        }
    }

    private Response handleSetTopicAttributes(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String topicArn = getParam(params, "TopicArn");
        String attributeName = getParam(params, "AttributeName");
        String attributeValue = getParam(params, "AttributeValue");
        try {
            snsService.setTopicAttributes(topicArn, attributeName, attributeValue, region);
            return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelopeNoResult("SetTopicAttributes", AwsNamespaces.SNS)).build();
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            return xmlErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage(), e.getHttpStatus());
        }
    }

    private Response handleSubscribe(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String topicArn = getParam(params, "TopicArn");
        String protocol = getParam(params, "Protocol");
        String endpoint = getParam(params, "Endpoint");
        try {
            Subscription sub = snsService.subscribe(topicArn, protocol, endpoint, region);

            String result = new XmlBuilder().elem("SubscriptionArn", sub.getSubscriptionArn()).build();
            return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("Subscribe", AwsNamespaces.SNS, result)).build();
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            return xmlErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage(), e.getHttpStatus());
        }
    }

    private Response handleUnsubscribe(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String subscriptionArn = getParam(params, "SubscriptionArn");
        try {
            snsService.unsubscribe(subscriptionArn, region);
            return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelopeNoResult("Unsubscribe", AwsNamespaces.SNS)).build();
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            return xmlErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage(), e.getHttpStatus());
        }
    }

    private Response handleListSubscriptions(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        List<Subscription> subs = snsService.listSubscriptions(region);
        return buildSubscriptionListResponse("ListSubscriptions", subs);
    }

    private Response handleListSubscriptionsByTopic(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String topicArn = getParam(params, "TopicArn");
        try {
            List<Subscription> subs = snsService.listSubscriptionsByTopic(topicArn, region);
            return buildSubscriptionListResponse("ListSubscriptionsByTopic", subs);
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            return xmlErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage(), e.getHttpStatus());
        }
    }

    private Response buildSubscriptionListResponse(String action, List<Subscription> subs) {
        var xml = new XmlBuilder().start("Subscriptions");
        for (Subscription s : subs) {
            xml.start("member")
               .elem("TopicArn", s.getTopicArn())
               .elem("Protocol", s.getProtocol())
               .elem("SubscriptionArn", s.getSubscriptionArn())
               .elem("Owner", s.getOwner() != null ? s.getOwner() : "")
               .elem("Endpoint", s.getEndpoint() != null ? s.getEndpoint() : "")
               .end("member");
        }
        xml.end("Subscriptions");
        return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope(action, AwsNamespaces.SNS, xml.build())).build();
    }

    private Response handlePublish(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String topicArn = getParam(params, "TopicArn");
        String targetArn = getParam(params, "TargetArn");
        String phoneNumber = getParam(params, "PhoneNumber");
        String message = getParam(params, "Message");
        String subject = getParam(params, "Subject");
        String messageGroupId = getParam(params, "MessageGroupId");
        String messageDeduplicationId = getParam(params, "MessageDeduplicationId");

        Map<String, String> attributes = new HashMap<>();
        for (int i = 1; ; i++) {
            String name = params.getFirst("MessageAttributes.entry." + i + ".Name");
            if (name == null) break;
            String value = params.getFirst("MessageAttributes.entry." + i + ".Value.StringValue");
            if (value != null) attributes.put(name, value);
        }

        try {
            String messageId = snsService.publish(topicArn, targetArn, phoneNumber, message, subject,
                    attributes, messageGroupId, messageDeduplicationId, region);

            String result = new XmlBuilder().elem("MessageId", messageId).build();
            return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("Publish", AwsNamespaces.SNS, result)).build();
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            return xmlErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage(), e.getHttpStatus());
        }
    }

    private Response handlePublishBatch(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String topicArn = getParam(params, "TopicArn");
        List<Map<String, Object>> entries = new ArrayList<>();
        for (int i = 1; ; i++) {
            String id = getParam(params, "PublishBatchRequestEntries.member." + i + ".Id");
            if (id == null) break;
            Map<String, Object> entry = new java.util.HashMap<>();
            entry.put("Id", id);
            entry.put("Message", getParam(params, "PublishBatchRequestEntries.member." + i + ".Message"));
            entry.put("Subject", getParam(params, "PublishBatchRequestEntries.member." + i + ".Subject"));
            entry.put("MessageGroupId", getParam(params, "PublishBatchRequestEntries.member." + i + ".MessageGroupId"));
            entry.put("MessageDeduplicationId", getParam(params, "PublishBatchRequestEntries.member." + i + ".MessageDeduplicationId"));
            entries.add(entry);
        }
        try {
            SnsService.BatchPublishResult result = snsService.publishBatch(topicArn, entries, region);

            var xml = new XmlBuilder().start("Successful");
            for (String[] s : result.successful()) {
                xml.start("member").elem("Id", s[0]).elem("MessageId", s[1]).end("member");
            }
            xml.end("Successful").start("Failed");
            for (String[] f : result.failed()) {
                xml.start("member").elem("Id", f[0]).elem("Code", f[1])
                   .elem("Message", f[2]).elem("SenderFault", f[3]).end("member");
            }
            xml.end("Failed");
            return Response.ok(AwsQueryResponse.envelope("PublishBatch", AwsNamespaces.SNS, xml.build())).build();
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            return xmlErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage(), e.getHttpStatus());
        }
    }

    private Response handleGetSubscriptionAttributes(MultivaluedMap<String, String> params, String region) {
        String subscriptionArn = getParam(params, "SubscriptionArn");
        try {
            Map<String, String> attrs = snsService.getSubscriptionAttributes(subscriptionArn, region);
            var xml = new XmlBuilder().start("Attributes");

     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * Fluent, allocation-efficient XML builder backed by a plain {@link StringBuilder}.
     5	 *
     6	 * <p>All content written via {@link #elem} and {@link #start} is automatically escaped.
     7	 * Pre-built XML fragments can be injected without re-escaping via {@link #raw}.
     8	 *
     9	 * <pre>{@code
    10	 * String xml = new XmlBuilder()
    11	 *     .start("CreateQueueResponse")
    12	 *       .start("CreateQueueResult")
    13	 *         .elem("QueueUrl", queue.getQueueUrl())
    14	 *       .end("CreateQueueResult")
    15	 *       .raw(AwsQueryResponse.responseMetadata())
    16	 *     .end("CreateQueueResponse")
    17	 *     .build();
    18	 * }</pre>
    19	 */
    20	public final class XmlBuilder {
    21	
    22	    private final StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
    23	
    24	    /** Opens {@code <element xmlns="xmlns">}. Omits the xmlns attribute when {@code xmlns} is null. */
    25	    public XmlBuilder start(String element, String xmlns) {
    26	        sb.append('<').append(element);
    27	        if (xmlns != null) {
    28	            sb.append(" xmlns=\"").append(xmlns).append('"');
    29	        }
    30	        sb.append('>');
    31	        return this;
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    /** Opens {@code <element>} without a namespace. */
    35	    public XmlBuilder start(String element) {
    36	        return start(element, null);
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    /** Appends {@code </element>}. */
    40	    public XmlBuilder end(String element) {
    41	        sb.append("</").append(element).append('>');
    42	        return this;
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    /**
    46	     * Appends {@code <name>escapedValue</name>}.
    47	     * Skips the element entirely when {@code value} is {@code null}.
    48	     */
    49	    public XmlBuilder elem(String name, String value) {
    50	        if (value == null) {
    51	            return this;
    52	        }
    53	        sb.append('<').append(name).append('>')
    54	          .append(escape(value))
    55	          .append("</").append(name).append('>');
    56	        return this;
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    /** Convenience overload — converts {@code long} to string. */
    60	    public XmlBuilder elem(String name, long value) {
    61	        return elem(name, String.valueOf(value));
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    /** Convenience overload — converts {@code boolean} to string. */
    65	    public XmlBuilder elem(String name, boolean value) {
    66	        return elem(name, String.valueOf(value));
    67	    }
    68	
    69	    /**
    70	     * Appends a pre-built XML fragment verbatim, without escaping.
    71	     * The caller is responsible for correctness of the fragment.
    72	     */
    73	    public XmlBuilder raw(String fragment) {
    74	        if (fragment != null) {
    75	            sb.append(fragment);
    76	        }
    77	        return this;
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    /** Returns the accumulated XML string. */
    81	    public String build() {
    82	        return sb.toString();
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    /**
    86	     * Escapes the five XML special characters: {@code & < > " '}.
    87	     * Returns an empty string for null or empty input.
    88	     */
    89	    public static String escape(String s) {
    90	        if (s == null || s.isEmpty()) {
    91	            return "";
    92	        }
    93	        StringBuilder out = null;
    94	        int len = s.length();
    95	        for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
    96	            char c = s.charAt(i);
    97	            String replacement = switch (c) {
    98	                case '&'  -> "&amp;";
    99	                case '<'  -> "&lt;";
   100	                case '>'  -> "&gt;";
   101	                case '"'  -> "&quot;";
   102	                case '\'' -> "&apos;";
   103	                default   -> null;
   104	            };
   105	            if (replacement != null) {
   106	                if (out == null) {
   107	                    out = new StringBuilder(len + 8);
   108	                    out.append(s, 0, i);
   109	                }
   110	                out.append(replacement);
   111	            } else if (out != null) {
   112	                out.append(c);
   113	            }
   114	        }
   115	        return out != null ? out.toString() : s;
   116	    }

cat > /tmp/repro_raw_delivery.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
LOG=/tmp/floci-repro.log
rm -f "$LOG"
java -jar target/quarkus-app/quarkus-run.jar >"$LOG" 2>&1 &
PID=$!
trap 'kill $PID >/dev/null 2>&1 || true' EXIT
for i in $(seq 1 60); do
  if curl -sS http://localhost:4566/ >/dev/null 2>&1; then break; fi
  sleep 1
  if ! kill -0 $PID >/dev/null 2>&1; then echo "server exited"; cat "$LOG"; exit 2; fi
  if [ "$i" = 60 ]; then echo "server failed to start"; cat "$LOG"; exit 2; fi
done
post() { curl -sS -X POST http://localhost:4566/ -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' --data-urlencode "$1" ${@:2}; }
TOPIC_XML=$(curl -sS -X POST http://localhost:4566/ -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' --data 'Action=CreateTopic&Name=repro-raw-topic')
TOPIC_ARN=$(echo "$TOPIC_XML" | sed -n 's:.*<TopicArn>\([^<]*\)</TopicArn>.*:\1:p')
curl -sS -X POST http://localhost:4566/ -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' --data 'Action=CreateQueue&QueueName=repro-raw-queue' >/dev/null
QUEUE_ARN='arn:aws:sqs:us-east-1:000000000000:repro-raw-queue'
SUB_XML=$(curl -sS -X POST http://localhost:4566/ -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' --data-urlencode Action=Subscribe --data-urlencode TopicArn="$TOPIC_ARN" --data-urlencode Protocol=sqs --data-urlencode Endpoint="$QUEUE_ARN")
SUB_ARN=$(echo "$SUB_XML" | sed -n 's:.*<SubscriptionArn>\([^<]*\)</SubscriptionArn>.*:\1:p')
curl -sS -X POST http://localhost:4566/ -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' --data-urlencode Action=SetSubscriptionAttributes --data-urlencode SubscriptionArn="$SUB_ARN" --data-urlencode AttributeName=RawMessageDelivery --data-urlencode AttributeValue=true >/dev/null
curl -sS -X POST http://localhost:4566/ -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' --data-urlencode Action=Publish --data-urlencode TopicArn="$TOPIC_ARN" --data-urlencode 'Message={"orderId":"123"}' >/dev/null
RECV_XML=$(curl -sS -X POST http://localhost:4566/ -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' --data-urlencode Action=ReceiveMessage --data-urlencode QueueUrl='http://localhost:4566/000000000000/repro-raw-queue')
echo "$RECV_XML"
BODY=$(echo "$RECV_XML" | sed -n 's:.*<Body>\(.*\)</Body>.*:\1:p' | sed 's/&quot;/"/g; s/&amp;/\&/g; s/&lt;/</g; s/&gt;/>/g; s/&apos;/'"'"'/g')
if [ "$BODY" = '{"orderId":"123"}' ]; then
  echo "PASS raw delivery"
else
  echo "FAIL expected raw body, got: $BODY" >&2
  exit 1
fi
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_raw_delivery.sh

cat > /tmp/repro_raw_delivery_direct.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cat > /tmp/ReproRawDelivery.java <<'JAVA'
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.RegionResolver;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.SnsService;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model.Topic;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model.Subscription;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sqs.SqsService;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sqs.model.Message;
import java.lang.reflect.Constructor;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

public class ReproRawDelivery {
  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    String region = "us-east-1";
    String account = "000000000000";
    String baseUrl = "http://localhost:4566";
    RegionResolver rr = new RegionResolver(region, account);

    Constructor<SqsService> sqsCtor = SqsService.class.getDeclaredConstructor(
        io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.StorageBackend.class,
        int.class, int.class, String.class);
    sqsCtor.setAccessible(true);
    SqsService sqs = sqsCtor.newInstance(new InMemoryStorage<>(), 30, 262144, baseUrl);
    sqs.createQueue("raw-queue", null, region);

    Constructor<SnsService> snsCtor = SnsService.class.getDeclaredConstructor(
        io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.StorageBackend.class,
        io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.StorageBackend.class,
        RegionResolver.class,
        SqsService.class,
        io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.lambda.LambdaService.class);
    snsCtor.setAccessible(true);
    SnsService sns = snsCtor.newInstance(new InMemoryStorage<>(), new InMemoryStorage<>(), rr, sqs, null);

    Topic topic = sns.createTopic("raw-topic", null, null, region);
    Subscription sub = sns.subscribe(topic.getTopicArn(), "sqs", "arn:aws:sqs:us-east-1:000000000000:raw-queue", region);
    sns.setSubscriptionAttribute(sub.getSubscriptionArn(), "RawMessageDelivery", "true", region);
    sns.publish(topic.getTopicArn(), null, null, "{\"orderId\":\"123\"}", null, Map.of(), region);

    List<Message> messages = sqs.receiveMessage(baseUrl + "/" + account + "/raw-queue", 1, 30, 0, region);
    if (messages.isEmpty()) throw new AssertionError("No SQS message delivered");
    String body = messages.get(0).getBody();
    System.out.println(body);
    if (!"{\"orderId\":\"123\"}".equals(body)) {
      throw new AssertionError("Expected raw body but got: " + body);
    }
  }
}
JAVA
CP="/testbed/target/classes:$(find /testbed/target/quarkus-app/lib -type f -name '*.jar' | tr '\n' ':')"
javac -cp "$CP" /tmp/ReproRawDelivery.java
java -cp "/tmp:$CP" ReproRawDelivery
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_raw_delivery_direct.sh

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cat > /tmp/ReproSnsSqsDeliveryModes.java <<'JAVA'
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.RegionResolver;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.SnsService;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model.Topic;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sns.model.Subscription;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sqs.SqsService;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.sqs.model.Message;
import java.lang.reflect.Constructor;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

public class ReproSnsSqsDeliveryModes {
  static final String REGION = "us-east-1";
  static final String ACCOUNT = "000000000000";
  static final String BASE_URL = "http://localhost:4566";

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    RegionResolver rr = new RegionResolver(REGION, ACCOUNT);
    Constructor<SqsService> sqsCtor = SqsService.class.getDeclaredConstructor(
        io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.StorageBackend.class,
        int.class, int.class, String.class);
    sqsCtor.setAccessible(true);
    SqsService sqs = sqsCtor.newInstance(new InMemoryStorage<>(), 30, 262144, BASE_URL);
    sqs.createQueue("raw-queue", null, REGION);
    sqs.createQueue("wrapped-queue", null, REGION);

    Constructor<SnsService> snsCtor = SnsService.class.getDeclaredConstructor(
        io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.StorageBackend.class,
        io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.StorageBackend.class,
        RegionResolver.class,
        SqsService.class,
        io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.lambda.LambdaService.class);
    snsCtor.setAccessible(true);
    SnsService sns = snsCtor.newInstance(new InMemoryStorage<>(), new InMemoryStorage<>(), rr, sqs, null);

    Topic topic = sns.createTopic("topic", null, null, REGION);
    Subscription rawSub = sns.subscribe(topic.getTopicArn(), "sqs", "arn:aws:sqs:us-east-1:000000000000:raw-queue", REGION);
    sns.setSubscriptionAttribute(rawSub.getSubscriptionArn(), "RawMessageDelivery", "true", REGION);
    sns.subscribe(topic.getTopicArn(), "sqs", "arn:aws:sqs:us-east-1:000000000000:wrapped-queue", REGION);

    sns.publish(topic.getTopicArn(), null, null, "{\"orderId\":\"123\"}", null, Map.of("eventType", "created"), REGION);

    String rawBody = receiveBody(sqs, "raw-queue");
    String wrappedBody = receiveBody(sqs, "wrapped-queue");
    System.out.println("raw=" + rawBody);
    System.out.println("wrapped=" + wrappedBody);

    if (!"{\"orderId\":\"123\"}".equals(rawBody)) throw new AssertionError("raw body was wrapped: " + rawBody);
    if (!wrappedBody.contains("\"Type\":\"Notification\"") || !wrappedBody.contains("\"Message\":\"{\\\"orderId\\\":\\\"123\\\"}\"")) {
      throw new AssertionError("default body was not SNS envelope: " + wrappedBody);
    }
  }

  static String receiveBody(SqsService sqs, String queueName) {
    List<Message> messages = sqs.receiveMessage(BASE_URL + "/" + ACCOUNT + "/" + queueName, 1, 30, 0, REGION);
    if (messages.isEmpty()) throw new AssertionError("No message in " + queueName);
    return messages.get(0).getBody();
  }
}
